It is important to note, the home warranty company you mention is Old Republic warranty co.  Per Old Republic policy, they only cover a regular water heater. In the County of Santa Barbara, everyone is required to install LoNox water heaters (due to emissions). This being a mobile home there is also a permit required by the state for $196. If an inspector catches someone without a permit the fine is double, $392. Any trustworthy plumber should bring the water heater up to current code to protect their client, as all code violations are the responsibility of the homeowner. It is highly unlikely that a licensed plumber would be able to install an up to code, permitted water heater for $200 (the permit itself being $196). <Text>Overall, a good church with plenty mass times to accommodate its parishioners in both English and Spanish.  I mostly attend the Sunday 11am mass with my Spanish speaking mother.  Love the chorus as it adds to the mass experience.  But much is left to be desired with regards to ill mannered teenagers and children who attend mass with their parents and who constantly talk and misbehave during mass.  Furthermore, now that we are returning to “normal”,  some parishioners of all ages flagrantly disregard the mask policy and the ushers don’t enforce it.  Some use their mask as chin straps or just cover their mouth and not their noses.  Science versus Faith - do you believe in a higher power to protect you from Covid19 being spread by disobedient parishioners or do you just stay home and pray the Lord will be understanding of your choice not to attend.  I find it hard to reconcile my feelings toward an institution grounded in so many rules and protocols who won’t enforce a simple mask mandate aimed to protect lives. I highly recommend this massage place. I get massages as part of my pain management regimen for two fractures in my lower spine.
My dad, mom and I booked our appointments together since we were going to be near by.
I had Hide, he was excellent at finding my problem areas with only the few sentences I said before the massage started. He adjusted the pressure to be strong for me. Also I have large breats and he was able adjust the massage table head rest to take some pressure off my chest when I was on my stomach.
My mom and dad both had Jessica. My dad has been having trouble with tingling and loss of sensation in his arm and hand. Jessica was able to get him back to 80% of his normal function during the hour massage, he feels much better. My mom has trouble with toxins from allergies gathering in her neck and shoulders, Jessica focused 70% of the massage on those areas when asked to and did a wonderful job.
We all would love to come again.</text>

< Review>
Fairly new to the area and we tried this spot since we always see it on the way to Costco. Ordered ahead and was given a time to pick up. Went in and asked if the order was read 5 minutes after the time I was told. They had not even started the order. My first time here and I have to say it's surprisingly good for what is essentially a fast food place.  :)

<UserId.>106359794720120539832</UserId.><name>Think Outside Your Boundaries< /name>< time>
1550985637890<//time>
<rating>4<//rating>< Text>
This is a great place if you want some fast teriyaki foods or rolls. It's kind of a fast food place for Japanese food. Taste-wise, the kids like most of the stuff, however they eat a lot of Japanese foods and still like the traditional sit down restaurants and would rather wait a bit for better tasting dishes.  They said the rice in rolls was on the hard side a d did not have enough vinegar. For the tempura items, the oil seemed a bit old and in need of change.

Pros: free parking; fast service; ample tables to sit at, but most people buy and go, store is pretty clean, and well lit; servers are friendly, and helpful (even making a special roll that was not on their menu; fish and meats are fresh; portions for the numbered combo are very big and one order can feed two; they also have a rewards program (ask about it, i.e. buy ten lion king rolls and get one free)

Cons: very limited open spaces, especially when the other stores next door are open; smoke fills up the restaurant; rolls don't have an authentic taste (fills the stomach and good, but flavor, size, and taste a little different); rice was a little harder than we liked it

We come here a few times a year, and it's best to keep it that way.  It's good when we need something fast.< /Text>
